	germanization_baltics = {

	claim_anatolia_byz = {
	picture = bicephalous_eagle
		potential = {
			tag = BYZ
			NOT = { has_country_flag = claim_anatolia_byz }
			has_country_flag = BYZ_borders
			has_country_flag = accept_armenians
			NOT = { has_country_flag = greek_pacifism }
		}

		allow = {
			BYZ = { is_greater_power = yes all_core = { owned_by = THIS } }
			invention = national_fraternity		
			nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
			war_policy = jingoism
			war = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = greek_pacifism }
		}

		effect = {
			prestige = 10
			badboy = 6
			set_country_flag = claim_anatolia_byz
			TUR_876 = { #Ankara 876 877 878 868
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_894 = { #Adana 894 896 898 895 900
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			900 = { #Antioch
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			898 = { #Antep
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			899 = { #Urfa
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_890 = { #Van
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_885 = { #Kars 885 886 1096
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_893 = { #Diyarbakir
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_887 = { #Erzurum
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_3435 = { #Harput
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			TUR_879 = { #Sivas
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			896 = { #Marash
				add_core = BYZ
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_culture_group = pan_greek }
				militancy = -1
				dominant_issue = { factor = 0.1 value = jingoism }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

			}

		}

			factor = 1
		}
	}

			has_country_flag = greece_has_got_a_brand_new_bag
			#GRE = { all_core = { owned_by = THIS } }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = claim_ikonion }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = greek_pacifism }

			set_country_flag = claim_ikonion

				dominant_issue = { factor = 0.1 value = jingoism }
			}
		}

		}
	}
